<div id="review_113193012" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/113193012" />
    <a title="K.D. Absolutely" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2156200-k-d-absolutely"><img alt="K.D. Absolutely" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471967140p2/2156200.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/113193012?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K.D. Absolutely" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K.D. Absolutely" href="/user/show/2156200-k-d-absolutely">K.D. Absolutely</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780763647513" href="/book/show/9876511-monsters-of-men">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to K.D. by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3404142-ace">Ace</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2156200-k-d-absolutely?shelf=borrowed">borrowed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2156200-k-d-absolutely?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2156200-k-d-absolutely?shelf=populist">populist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2156200-k-d-absolutely?shelf=war">war</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2156200-k-d-absolutely?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer113193012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15579923969061056357">YA fantasy at its finest.<br/><br/>The best book in this trilogy. What a way to conclude the story.<br/><br/>This is the LOTR of the 21st century. The triumph of good over evil is a deathless theme and no matter how many times it has been written, during our times of uncertainties, hope is sometimes the only thing that remains with us to hold on to. <br/><br/>I loved everything about it. Well, to do that, I had to drop all my defenses, sit back and relax and let myself be wooed by Ness. When I decided to crack this final boo</span>
  <span id="freeText15579923969061056357" style="display:none">YA fantasy at its finest.<br /><br />The best book in this trilogy. What a way to conclude the story.<br /><br />This is the LOTR of the 21st century. The triumph of good over evil is a deathless theme and no matter how many times it has been written, during our times of uncertainties, hope is sometimes the only thing that remains with us to hold on to. <br /><br />I loved everything about it. Well, to do that, I had to drop all my defenses, sit back and relax and let myself be wooed by Ness. When I decided to crack this final book open, I said to myself that since this is the last one, I would not be too hard on myself and read this, and try to forget how good Gabriel Garcia Marquez in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23887.The_Autumn_of_the_Patriarch" title="The Autumn of the Patriarch by Gabriel Garcí­a Márquez" rel="nofollow noopener">The Autumn of the Patriarch</a> (also 4 stars). Well, obviously Ness does not compare <i>I am biased</i> to Garcia Marquez but in the first place, I think it is unfair to compare them because they came from different parts of the world, began writing at different times and write books in totally different genres.<br /><br />But good writing is good writing no matter in what genre the book belongs. Also, this book, <i>Monsters of Man</i>, even the whole series for that matter, is not just even good. The writing of Patrick Ness is youngishly innovative as his <i>imaginayshun</i> is boundless. I have not seen anything like his writing. The world that he created is not as extensive as the Middle Earth of Tolkien but interesting enough for me to continue and finish the whole trilogy. The ability of some of the characters to hear thoughts has been tackled by Lois Lowry but the way Ness used that here is more extensive and satisfying.<br /><br />I enjoyed this better than the 2 books that I so far read that are included in the <i>A Song of Fire and Ice</i> (another YA series that I've decided to complete before I die). The reason is that Patrick Ness knows how to elicit strong emotions from his readers <i>and to think that there is no sex here.</i> Not only the love-hate <i>I'm too old for this</i> multidimensional relationship of <b>Todd</b> and <b>Viola</b> but also delivering a reminder to all of us that <u>
  <b>war makes monsters out of men.</b>
</u> War is stupid. Period.<br /><br />This book is a YA but it does not insult adult's intelligence even sensibilities. The plot, conflicts, climax and denouement are all plausible. You just have to let loose while you are reading. Drop all your defenses. Probably like how I imagine myself if I were to have sex with a prostitute <i>not that I've ever tried</i> - I have just to lie down and let her do all the works. It's good that my wife is not here on Goodreads.<br /><br />My favorite characters are <b>The Source</b> and <b>Mistress Coyle.</b> Well, I always love characters that are in the gray zone: not really a villain but not really a hero and in both roles they could do things on the extremes: really bad when they play the villain role and really angelic (my impression) when they play the hero role. I was also pleasantly surprised when Ness used a third narrator <b>1017</b> in this book. It heightened the beauty of the whole narrative by having us see the brilliant unfolding of the events with a fresh set of eyes, i.e., fresh voice.<br /><br />If all YAs are like this, I will not mind having to read books written for teens when I am in my twilight years. I won't even mind having books by Patrick Ness in my deathbed.<br /><br />Patrick Ness rules!<br /><br />Ace Jose rocks!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15579923969061056357" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_8811134'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8811134-fear"><img alt="Fear (Gone, #5)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1309186708l/8811134._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rhDVeacZeTGyFFrdVOWkZ6mYKi5eAWw5lYecv7wLamSn8t5YPE0J513PkjG3f6U0/suO5B64YiNN1pZmxA0DKg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mK1VQUtZYParOgMwLh3DujVnkbketWug/84b71sJVZSRT15g0A0QIEThy9zNh8LpYjQ1c14MZbonnxE2Iw882g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10571641211966284835">Patrick Ness, an award-winning novelist, has written for England’s Radio 4 and <i>Sunday Telegraph</i> and is a literary critic for <i>The Guardian</i>. He has written many books, including the <i>Chaos Walking Trilogy</i>, <i>The Crash of Hennington</i>, <i>Topics About Which I Know Nothing</i>, and <i>A Monster Calls</i>. <br/> <br/>He has won numerous awards, including the Guardian Children’s Fiction Prize, the Booktrust Teenage Prize, and the C</span>
  <span id="freeText10571641211966284835" style="display:none">Patrick Ness, an award-winning novelist, has written for England’s Radio 4 and <i>Sunday Telegraph</i> and is a literary critic for <i>The Guardian</i>. He has written many books, including the <i>Chaos Walking Trilogy</i>, <i>The Crash of Hennington</i>, <i>Topics About Which I Know Nothing</i>, and <i>A Monster Calls</i>. <br /> <br />He has won numerous awards, including the Guardian Children’s Fiction Prize, the Booktrust Teenage Prize, and the Costa Children’s Book Award. Born in Virginia, he currently lives in London. </span>
